ValidateInitialization ensures an authorizer is set.\n   127→func (s *Plugin) ValidateInitialization() error {\n   128→\tif s.client == nil {\n   129→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"missing client\")\n   130→\t}\n   131→\tif s.serviceAccountLister == nil {\n   132→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"missing serviceAccountLister\")\n   133→\t}\n   134→\treturn nil\n   135→}\n   136→\n   137→// Admit verifies if the pod should be admitted\n   138→func (s *Plugin) Admit(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces) (err error) {\n   139→\tif shouldIgnore(a) {\n   140→\t\treturn nil\n   141→\t}\n   142→\tif a.GetOperation() != admission.Create {\n   143→\t\t// we only mutate pods during create requests\n   144→\t\treturn nil\n   145→\t}\n   146→\tpod := a.GetObject().(*api.Pod)\n   147→\n   148→\t// Don't modify the spec of mirror pods.\n   149→\t// That makes the kubelet very angry and confused, and it immediately deletes the pod (because the spec doesn't match)\n   150→\t// That said, don't allow mirror pods to reference ServiceAccounts or SecretVolumeSources either\n   151→\tif _, isMirrorPod := pod.Annotations[api.MirrorPodAnnotationKey]; isMirrorPod {\n   152→\t\treturn s.Validate(ctx, a, o)\n   153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\t// Set the default service account if needed\n   156→\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) == 0 {\n   157→\t\tpod.Spec.ServiceAccountName = DefaultServiceAccountName\n   158→\t}\n   159→\n   160→\tserviceAccount, err := s.getServiceAccount(a.GetNamespace(), pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName)\n   161→\tif err != nil {\n   162→\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"error looking up service account %s/%s: %w\", a.GetNamespace(), pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName, err))\n   163→\t}\n   164→\tif s.MountServiceAccountToken && shouldAutomount(serviceAccount, pod) {\n   165→\t\ts.mountServiceAccountToken(serviceAccount, pod)\n   166→\t}\n   167→\tif len(pod.Spec.ImagePullSecrets) == 0 {\n   168→\t\tpod.Spec.ImagePullSecrets = make([]api.LocalObjectReference, len(serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets))\n   169→\t\tfor i := 0; i < len(serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets); i++ {\n   170→\t\t\tpod.Spec.ImagePullSecrets[i].Name = serviceAccount.ImagePullSecrets[i].Name\n   171→\t\t}\n   172→\t}\n   173→\n   174→\treturn s.Validate(ctx, a, o)\n   175→}\n   176→\n   177→// Validate the data we obtained\n   178→func (s *Plugin) Validate(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces) (err error) {\n   179→\tif shouldIgnore(a) {\n   180→\t\treturn nil\n   181→\t}\n   182→\n   183→\tpod := a.GetObject().(*api.Pod)\n   184→\n   185→\tif a.GetOperation() == admission.Update && a.GetSubresource() == \"ephemeralcontainers\" {\n   186→\t\treturn s.limitEphemeralContainerSecretReferences(pod, a)\n   187→\t}\n   188→\n   189→\tif a.GetOperation() != admission.Create {\n   190→\t\t// we only validate pod specs during create requests\n   191→\t\treturn nil\n   192→\t}\n   193→\n   194→\t// Mirror pods have restrictions on what they can reference\n   195→\tif _, isMirrorPod := pod.Annotations[api.MirrorPodAnnotationKey]; isMirrorPod {\n   196→\t\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) != 0 {\n   197→\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"a mirror pod may not reference service accounts\"))\n   198→\t\t}\n   199→\t\thasSecrets := false\n   200→\t\tpodutil.VisitPodSecretNames(pod, func(name string) bool {\n   201→\t\t\thasSecrets = true\n   202→\t\t\treturn false\n   203→\t\t}, podutil.AllContainers)\n   204→\t\tif hasSecrets {\n   205→\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"a mirror pod may not reference secrets\"))\n   206→\t\t}\n   207→\t\tfor _, v := range pod.Spec.Volumes {\n   208→\t\t\tif proj := v.Projected; proj != nil {\n   209→\t\t\t\tfor _, projSource := range proj.Sources {\n   210→\t\t\t\t\tif projSource.ServiceAccountToken != nil {\n   211→\t\t\t\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"a mirror pod may not use ServiceAccountToken volume projections\"))\n   212→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   213→\t\t\t\t}\n   214→\t\t\t}\n   215→\t\t}\n   216→\t\treturn nil\n   217→\t}\n   218→\n   219→\t// Require container pods to have service accounts\n   220→\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) == 0 {\n   221→\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"no service account specified for pod %s/%s\", a.GetNamespace(), pod.Name))\n   222→\t}\n   223→\t// Ensure the referenced service account exists\n   224→\tserviceAccount, err := s.getServiceAccount(a.GetNamespace(), pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName)\n   225→\tif err != nil {\n   226→\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"error looking up service account %s/%s: %v\", a.GetNamespace(), pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName, err))\n   227→\t}\n   228→\n   229→\tif s.enforceMountableSecrets(serviceAccount) {\n   230→\t\tif err := s.limitSecretReferences(serviceAccount, pod); err != nil {\n   231→\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, err)\n   232→\t\t}\n   233→\t}\n   234→\n   235→\treturn nil\n   236→}\n   237→\n   238→func shouldIgnore(a admission.Attributes) bool {\n   239→\tif a.GetResource().GroupResource() != api.Resource(\"pods\") || (a.GetSubresource() != \"\" && a.GetSubresource() != \"ephemeralcontainers\") {\n   240→\t\treturn true\n   241→\t}\n   242→\tobj := a.GetObject()\n   243→\tif obj == nil {\n   244→\t\treturn true\n   245→\t}\n   246→\t_, ok := obj.(*api.Pod)\n   247→\tif !ok {\n   248→\t\treturn true\n   249→\t}\n   250→\n   251→\treturn false\n   252→}\n   253→\n   254→func shouldAutomount(sa *corev1.ServiceAccount, pod *api.Pod) bool {\n   255→\t// Pod's preference wins\n   256→\tif pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken != nil {\n   257→\t\treturn *pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken\n   258→\t}\n   259→\t// Then service account's\n   260→\tif sa.AutomountServiceAccountToken != nil {\n   261→\t\treturn *sa.AutomountServiceAccountToken\n   262→\t}\n   263→\t// Default to true for backwards compatibility\n   264→\treturn true\n   265→}\n   266→\n   267→// enforceMountableSecrets indicates whether mountable secrets should be enforced for a particular service account\n   268→// A global setting of true will override any flag set on the individual service account\n   269→func (s *Plugin) enforceMountableSecrets(serviceAccount *corev1.ServiceAccount) bool {\n   270→\tif s.LimitSecretReferences {\n   271→\t\treturn true\n   272→\t}\n   273→\n   274→\tif value, ok := serviceAccount.Annotations[EnforceMountableSecretsAnnotation]; ok {\n   275→\t\tenforceMountableSecretCheck, _ := strconv.ParseBool(value)\n   276→\t\treturn enforceMountableSecretCheck\n   277→\t}\n   278→\n   279→\treturn false\n   280→}\n   281→\n   282→// getServiceAccount returns the ServiceAccount for the given namespace and name if it exists\n   283→func (s *Plugin) getServiceAccount(namespace string, name string) (*corev1.ServiceAccount, error) {\n   284→\tserviceAccount, err := s.serviceAccountLister.ServiceAccounts(namespace).Get(name)\n   285→\tif err == nil {\n   286→\t\treturn serviceAccount, nil\n   287→\t}\n   288→\tif !errors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   289→\t\treturn nil, err\n   290→\t}\n   291→\n   292→\t// Could not find in cache, attempt to look up directly\n   293→\tnumAttempts := 1\n   294→\tif name == DefaultServiceAccountName {\n   295→\t\t// If this is the default serviceaccount, attempt more times, since it should be auto-created by the controller\n   296→\t\tnumAttempts = 10\n   297→\t}\n   298→\tretryInterval := time.Duration(rand.Int63n(100)+int64(100)) * time.Millisecond\n   299→\tfor i := 0; i < numAttempts; i++ {\n   300→\t\tif i != 0 {\n   301→\t\t\ttime.Sleep(retryInterval)\n   302→\t\t}\n   303→\t\tserviceAccount, err := s.client.CoreV1().ServiceAccounts(namespace).Get(context.TODO(), name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   304→\t\tif err == nil {\n   305→\t\t\treturn serviceAccount, nil\n   306→\t\t}\n   307→\t\tif !errors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   308→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   309→\t\t}\n   310→\t}\n   311→\n   312→\treturn nil, errors.NewNotFound(api.Resource(\"serviceaccount\"), name)\n   313→}\n   314→\n   315→func (s *Plugin) limitSecretReferences(serviceAccount *corev1.ServiceAccount, pod *api.Pod) 319→\t\tmountableSecrets.Insert(s.Name)\n   320→\t}\n   321→\tfor _, volume := range pod.Spec.Volumes {\n   322→\t\tsource := volume.VolumeSource\n   323→\t\tif source.Secret == nil {\n envFrom referencing secret.secretName=\\\"%s\\\" is not allowed because service account %s does not reference that secret\", container.Name, envFrom.SecretRef.Name, serviceAccount.Name)\n   344→\t\t\t\t}\n   345→\t\t\t}\n   346→\t\t}\n   347→\t}\n   348→\n   349→\tfor _, container := range pod.Spec.Containers {\n   350→\t\tfor _, env := range container.Env {\n   351→\t\t\tif %s referencing secret.secretName=\\\"%s\\\" is not allowed because service account %s does not reference that secret\", container.Name, env.Name, env.ValueFrom.SecretKeyRef.Name, serviceAccount.Name)\n   354→\t\t\t\t}\n   355→\t\t\t}\n   356→\t\t}\n   357→\t\tfor _, envFrom := range container.EnvFrom {\n   358→\t\t\tif envFrom.SecretRef != nil {\n   359→\t\t\t\tif not reference that secret\", container.Name, envFrom.SecretRef.Name, serviceAccount.Name)\n   361→\t\t\t\t}\n   362→\t\t\t}\n   363→\t\t}\n   364→\t}\n   365→\n   366→\t// limit pull secret references 479→\t\t\t},\n   480→\t\t})\n   481→\t}\n   482→}\n   483→\n   484→// TokenVolumeSource returns the projected volume source for service account token.\n   485→func TokenVolumeSource() nil\n\t})\n}\n\nvar _ = admission.Interface(&Plugin{})\n\n// Plugin contains the client used by the admission controller\ntype Plugin struct {\n\t*admission.Handler\n\n\t// LimitSecretReferences rejects pods that reference secrets their service accounts do not reference\n\tLimitSecretReferences bool\n\t// MountServiceAccountToken creates Volume and VolumeMounts for the first referenced ServiceAccountToken for the pod's service account\n\tMountServiceAccountToken bool\n\n\tclient kubernetes.Interface\n\n\tserviceAccountLister corev1listers.ServiceAccountLister\n\n\tgenerateName func(string) string\n}\n\nvar _ admission.MutationInterface = &Plugin{}\nvar _ admission.ValidationInterface = &Plugin{}\nvar _ = genericadmissioninitializer.WantsExternalKubeClientSet(&Plugin{})\nvar _ = genericadmissioninitializer.WantsExternalKubeInformerFactory(&Plugin{})\n\n// NewServiceAccount returns an admission.Interface implementation which limits admission of Pod CREATE requests based on the pod's ServiceAccount:\n// 1. If the pod does not specify a ServiceAccount, it sets the pod's ServiceAccount to \"default\"\n// 2. It ensures the ServiceAccount referenced by the pod exists\n// 3. If LimitSecretReferences is true, it rejects the pod if the pod references Secret objects which the pod's ServiceAccount does not reference\n// 4. If the pod does not contain any ImagePullSecrets, the ImagePullSecrets of the service account are added.\n// 5. If MountServiceAccountToken is true, it adds a VolumeMount with the pod's ServiceAccount's api token secret to containers\nfunc NewServiceAccount() *Plugin {\n\treturn &Plugin{\n\t\tHandler: admission.NewHandler(admission.Create, admission.Update),\n\t\t// TODO: enable this once we've swept secret usage to account for adding secret references to service accounts\n\t\tLimitSecretReferences: false,\n\t\t// Auto mount service account API token secrets\n\t\tMountServiceAccountToken: true,\n\n\t\tgenerateName: names.SimpleNameGenerator.GenerateName,\n\t}\n}\n\n// SetExternalKubeClientSet sets the client for the plugin\nfunc (s *Plugin) SetExternalKubeClientSet(cl kubernetes.Interface) {\n\ts.client = cl\n}\n\n// SetExternalKubeInformerFactory registers informers with the plugin\nfunc (s *Plugin) SetExternalKubeInformerFactory(f informers.SharedInformerFactory) {\n\tserviceAccountInformer := f.Core().V1().ServiceAccounts()\n\ts.serviceAccountLister = serviceAccountInformer.Lister()\n\ts.SetReadyFunc(func() bool {\n\t\treturn serviceAccountInformer.Informer().HasSynced()\n\t})\n}\n\n// ValidateInitialization ensures an authorizer is set.\nfunc (s *Plugin) ValidateInitialization() error {\n\tif s.client == nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"missing client\")\n\t}\n\tif s.serviceAccountLister == nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"missing serviceAccountLister\")\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Admit verifies if the pod should be admitted\nfunc (s *Plugin) Admit(ctx context.Context, a admission.Attributes, o admission.ObjectInterfaces) (err error) {\n\tif shouldIgnore(a) {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tif a.GetOperation() != admission.Create {\n\t\t// we only mutate pods during create requests\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tpod := a.GetObject().(*api.Pod)\n\n\t// Don't modify the spec of mirror pods.\n\t// That makes the kubelet very angry and confused, and it immediately deletes the pod (because the spec doesn't match)\n\t// That said, don't allow mirror pods to reference ServiceAccounts or SecretVolumeSources either\n\tif _, isMirrorPod := pod.Annotations[api.MirrorPodAnnotationKey]; isMirrorPod {\n\t\treturn s.Validate(ctx, a, o)\n\t}\n\n\t// Set the default service account if needed\n\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) == 0 admission.ObjectInterfaces) (err error) {\n\tif shouldIgnore(a) {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tpod := a.GetObject().(*api.Pod)\n\n\tif a.GetOperation() == admission.Update && a.GetSubresource() == \"ephemeralcontainers\" {\n\t\treturn s.limitEphemeralContainerSecretReferences(pod, a)\n\t}\n\n\tif a.GetOperation() != admission.Create {\n\t\t// we only validate pod specs during create requests\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Mirror pods have restrictions on what they can reference\n\tif _, isMirrorPod := pod.Annotations[api.MirrorPodAnnotationKey]; isMirrorPod {\n\t\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) != 0 {\n\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"a mirror pod may not reference service accounts\"))\n\t\t}\n\t\thasSecrets := false\n\t\tpodutil.VisitPodSecretNames(pod, func(name string) bool {\n\t\t\thasSecrets = true\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}, podutil.AllContainers)\n\t\tif hasSecrets {\n\t\t\treturn projSource := range proj.Sources {\n\t\t\t\t\tif projSource.ServiceAccountToken != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"a mirror pod may not use ServiceAccountToken volume projections\"))\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Require container pods to have service accounts\n\tif len(pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName) == 0 {\n\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"no service account specified for pod %s/%s\", a.GetNamespace(), pod.Name))\n\t}\n\t// Ensure the referenced service account exists\n\tserviceAccount, err := s.getServiceAccount(a.GetNamespace(), pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, fmt.Errorf(\"error looking up service account %s/%s: %v\", a.GetNamespace(), pod.Spec.ServiceAccountName, err))\n\t}\n\n\tif s.enforceMountableSecrets(serviceAccount) {\n\t\tif err := s.limitSecretReferences(serviceAccount, pod); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn admission.NewForbidden(a, err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc shouldIgnore(a admission.Attributes) bool {\n\tif a.GetResource().GroupResource() != api.Resource(\"pods\") || (a.GetSubresource() true\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc shouldAutomount(sa *corev1.ServiceAccount, pod *api.Pod) bool {\n\t// Pod's preference wins\n\tif pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken != nil {\n\t\treturn *pod.Spec.AutomountServiceAccountToken\n\t}\n\t// Then service account's\n\tif sa.AutomountServiceAccountToken != nil {\n\t\treturn *sa.AutomountServiceAccountToken\n\t}\n\t// Default to true for *api.Pod) error {\n\t// Ensure all secrets the pod references are allowed by the service account\n\tmountableSecrets := sets.NewString()\n\tfor _, s := range serviceAccount.Secrets nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Plugin) limitEphemeralContainerSecretReferences(pod *api.Pod, a admission.Attributes) error {\n\t// Require ephemeral container pods to have service accounts\n\tif components:\\n\\n1. **Admission Controller (Injection)**: The `plugin/pkg/admission/serviceaccount/admission.go` file contains the ServiceAccount admission plugin that automatically injects service account tokens into pods. The `Admit()` method calls `shouldAutomount()` to check if the pod's `AutomountServiceAccountToken` field or the service account's `AutomountServiceAccountToken` field indicate that token mounting is desired. If mounting should happen, `mountServiceAccountToken()` is called, which uses `TokenVolumeSource()` to create a projected volume with the service account token, CA certificate, and namespace information. The controller watches service account and secret resources, and through `syncSecret()` and `syncServiceAccount()` methods, it ensures that each service account has an associated token secret. The token secret contains the actual bearer token needed for API authentication.\\n\\n3. **Service Account Controller**: The `pkg/controller/serviceaccount/serviceaccounts_controller.go` creates default service accounts in new namespaces, ensuring these service accounts exist before pods try to use them.\\n\\n4. **Legacy Token Cleaner**: The `pkg/controller/serviceaccount/legacy_serviceaccount_token_cleaner.go` is responsible for cleaning up old, unused legacy service account token secrets based on their last usage time.\\n\\n5. **Token REST API**: The `pkg/registry/core/serviceaccount/storage/token.go` handles the TokenRequest API which provides bound tokens with expiration times (defined by `WarnOnlyBoundTokenExpirationSeconds` in `pkg/serviceaccount/claims.go`).\\n\\n6. **API Definitions**: The `AutomountServiceAccountToken` field is defined in both `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (for PodSpec and ServiceAccount) and `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (internal types). The token secret contains the actual bearer token needed for API authentication.\\n\\n3. **Service Account Controller**: The `pkg/controller/serviceaccount/serviceaccounts_controller.go` creates default service accounts in new namespaces, ensuring these service accounts exist before pods try to use them.\\n\\n4. **Legacy Token Cleaner**: The `pkg/controller/serviceaccount/legacy_serviceaccount_token_cleaner.go` is responsible for cleaning up old, unused legacy service account token secrets based on their last usage time.\\n\\n5. **Token REST API**: The `pkg/registry/core/serviceaccount/storage/token.go` handles the TokenRequest API which provides bound tokens with expiration times (defined by `WarnOnlyBoundTokenExpirationSeconds` in `pkg/serviceaccount/claims.go`).\\n\\n6. **API Definitions**: The `AutomountServiceAccountToken` field is defined in both `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go` (for PodSpec and ServiceAccount) and `pkg/apis/core/types.go` (internal types). The field is a boolean pointer that allows three states: true (mount), false (don't mount), or nil (use default).\\n\\n7. **Pod Spec Validation**: The `pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go` contains the `ValidatePodSpec()` function that validates pod specifications, including service account name validation, though it does not explicitly validate the `AutomountServiceAccountToken` field itself as it is a simple boolean pointer.\\n\\n8. **Client Apply Configurations**: The `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/applyconfigurations/core/v1/podspec.go` and `staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/applyconfigurations/core/v1/serviceaccount.go` provide structured apply configurations for clients to manage these fields.\\n\\nThe complete flow is: Pod creation → Admission controller evaluates `shouldAutomount()` based on pod and service account settings → If mounting is needed, `mountServiceAccountToken()` injects a projected volume → Token controller ensures the token secret exists and is kept in sync → TokenREST provides API for requesting bound tokens with expiration.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
